2025-10-23T01:24:13.5928607Z [36;1m[0m
2025-10-23T01:24:13.5928947Z [36;1m# The following logic implements the configuration priority described in the README:[0m

2025-10-23T01:24:13.5931470Z [36;1m# if the caller doesn't provide them, thus if the input matches the default we don't set it as we[0m
